This caused the guests to rush around repeatedly at the front desk, the executive lounge on the 28th floor, and the guest room floor. The experience was Extremely poor. Second, the hardware is poor. There is no waiting area in the lobby on the second floor and there are only 3 simple benches. There is no high-speed elevator, and the waiting time for high-rise rooms to go up and down the elevator is slow. The most unacceptable thing is to find poop in the hotel swimming pool! ****! ****! At 4:30 pm on the day of check-in, a family of friends who were swimming together in the hotel pool discovered something suspicious in the pool. It was confirmed at close range that it was feces! It means that all the family, children and friends in the swimming pool "drink" the fecal water! What‚Äôs even more disgusting is that if such a serious safety incident occurs, shouldn‚Äôt a Marriott-level five-star hotel immediately waterproof and disinfect it thoroughly before opening it to the public? Not really! The hotel reopened to the public that night after cleaning up the poop. Guests after the 5th used swimming pool water full of E. coli and Staphylococcus aureus! Is it disgusting? Is it surprising?
It can be said that the occurrence of feces was an accident. Marriott hotel staff, maintenance personnel, and lifeguards could not detect it. The hotel's SOP was ineffective and the subsequent rectification was extremely perfunctory. How to explain it?
The beautiful Marriott is black all his life! I belong to one of the top 100 multinational companies in the United States. I have asked the company's HR to terminate the agreement with Marriott next year and will not accept any Shunde suppliers from now on. It's so disappointing and terrible.
